
CREATE TABLE ['PO Transactions$'] (

	[Project Name] NVARCHAR(255) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[Project Desc] NVARCHAR(255) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[VAT] NVARCHAR(255) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[STATUS] NVARCHAR(255) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[Check No#] NVARCHAR(255) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[Date] DATETIME NULL, 
	[Payment] MONEY NULL, 
	[DEPOST PERC] FLOAT(53) NULL,

	[Comment 2] MONEY NULL, 
	[Comment 3] MONEY NULL, 
	[Comment 4] MONEY NULL,

)

CREATE TABLE [InventoryItems] (
	[InventoryItemUniqueId] INTEGER NOT NULL IDENTITY(1,1), 
	[Id] UNIQUEIDENTIFIER NOT NULL, 
	[Code] INTEGER NULL, 
	[SKU] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[EnName] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[ArName] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[ArEnName] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[StorageMethod] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[StorageUnit] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[BoxQtyTotal] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[QtyBoxTotal] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[WeightTotal] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[BoxQtyTotalCounter] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[QtyBoxTotalCounter] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[WeightTotalCounter] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[IngredientUnit] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[IngredientPrice] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[IngredientQty] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[MinQty] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[RequestQty] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[ParQty] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[MaxQty] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[CreatedAt] DATETIME2 NULL, 
	[UpdateAt] DATETIME2 NULL, 
	[AddedBy] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[AddedById] INTEGER NULL, 
	[ItemImg] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[MinPrice] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[MaxPrice] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[AveragePrice] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[CategoryName] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[CategoryId] INTEGER NULL, 
	[InventoryGeneralItemId] INTEGER NULL, 
	[InventoryName] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[InventoryId] INTEGER NULL, 
	[BoxQtyTotalInitial] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[QtyBoxTotalInitial] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[WeightTotalInitial] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	CONSTRAINT [PK_InventoryItems] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED ([InventoryItemUniqueId]), 
	CONSTRAINT [FK_InventoryItems_CafeItemCategories_CategoryId] FOREIGN KEY([CategoryId]) REFERENCES [CafeItemCategories] ([Id]), 
	CONSTRAINT [FK_InventoryItems_Inventories_InventoryId] FOREIGN KEY([InventoryId]) REFERENCES [Inventories] ([Id]), 
	CONSTRAINT [FK_InventoryItems_InventoryItemGenerals_InventoryGeneralItemId] FOREIGN KEY([InventoryGeneralItemId]) REFERENCES [InventoryItemGenerals] ([InventoryItemId])
)

CREATE TABLE [InventoryRequestsItems] (
	[RequestItemId] INTEGER NOT NULL IDENTITY(1,1), 
	[ArEnName] NVARCHAR(max) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL, 
	[BoxQtyTotal] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[QtyBoxTotal] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[WeightTotal] DECIMAL(18, 2) NULL, 
	[ExpDate] DATETIME2 NULL, 
	[CreatedAt] DATETIME2 NULL, 
	[InventoryGeneralItemId] INTEGER NULL, 
	[InventoryItemId] INTEGER NULL, 
	[InventoryRequestId] INTEGER NULL, 
	[PurchaseProofItemId] INTEGER NULL, 
	CONSTRAINT [PK_InventoryRequestsItems] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED ([RequestItemId]), 
	CONSTRAINT [FK_InventoryRequestsItems_InventoryItems_InventoryItemId] FOREIGN KEY([InventoryItemId]) REFERENCES [InventoryItems] ([InventoryItemUniqueId]), 
	CONSTRAINT [FK_InventoryRequestsItems_InventoryRequests_InventoryRequestId] FOREIGN KEY([InventoryRequestId]) REFERENCES [InventoryRequests] ([RequestId]), 
	CONSTRAINT [FK_InventoryRequestsItems_PurchaseProofItems_PurchaseProofItemId] FOREIGN KEY([PurchaseProofItemId]) REFERENCES [PurchaseProofItems] ([Id])
)

/*
